  404. I bought this so that I could cut my husband's hair. He was going to a local hair shop and dropping $20 every 3-4 weeks. He has very little hair, but it grows fast. His hair is fine and sparse, and he likes it cut very short - almost like a military cut. I *think* the clipper kit was supposed to come with a video, but it didn't so I logged on to YouTube and watched several hair cutting videos including ones specifically detailing using the Wahl clipper. After my education, I got to work on my first haircut which turned out stellar. My husband really liked it, and I have to say not only was it easy, it was fun.<br /><br />To be safe, I started out using the number 3 guide, which cuts the hair a bit longer. As always, start out by cutting less hair. You can always cut more as you go along. Once you have a feel for the guide you're using, it will be very easy to decide whether to go up or down a number. The number 3 guide helped me to get a feel for how the clipper performs, as well as the technique I should use. As the videos suggest, always use a rocking motion when running the guide through the hair. Never push down or allow the guide to settle in one place too long. Always keep it moving.<br /><br />Guides with higher numbers leave the hair longer. Guides with lower numbers are great for shorter haircuts. Again, if you want the hair to be very short, guides 2 and 3 are perfect. Also, to fine tune a straight edge along the back above the neck, you can use the clipper without any guide combs attached. I believe there is also an attachment for around the ears, but I used the clipper sans guides for that as well. So far with just 2 haircuts, this thing has pretty much paid for itself.<br /><br />The clipper is a bit heavier as other reviewers have commented, but that doesn't bother me. I don't consider it noisy. The on/off switch is solid, and you'll hear a resounding *click* each time you turn it on and off.<br /><br />A wonderful purchase to be sure. I highly recommend!

  611. I initially wrote a review of this product giving it 3 stars because I thought it was used. But upon reading some comments in the reviews section, I found someone complaining about the same thing and when I looked at the reply to that review. A wahl's representative said that the shavings aren't someone's hair but it is the shavings of the blade guard rubbing up against it during shipment. I believe it because when I saw the shavings on the blade initially I looked at it closely and it didn't really look like someone's hair nor did it have the texture of hair. I'm glad I came to the review section instead of just returning it. As for the quality of the product. The shipping cost to get the unit shipped back was double to what I paid for the unit, and I wasn't prepared to take a chance on getting my money back.
